RATIONALE: compounding punishes variance quadratically (gâ‰ˆخ¼âˆ’دƒآ²/2; leverage scales خ¼âˆ‌L but دƒآ²âˆ‌Lآ²) â†’ a +EV strategy at too-high leverage has NEGATIVE compound growth; fat gap-tail + correlated-dump pulls growth-optimal leverage below 20أ—; as stakes get real, shift growth-max â†’ ruin-aversion (fractional Kelly). Ties to scaling roadmap (ruin risk = binding constraint).
  - **ًں“گ v3 OPERATING PLAN (2026-07-02, operator-ratified â€” SUPERSEDES the 07-01 11-tier G/L design AND the guess tiers): working-capital reserve = PRIMARY (âœ… BUILT 2026-07-02), coarse 4-tier lev schedule = backstop.** Architecture: slippage/capacity = per-pair 0.1% cap + $500k ceiling (adaptive, the TRUE capacity governor â€” a global gross target was the wrong tool, operator-corrected); ruin = `reserve_mode="working_capital"` + `working_capital_target` (tradeable = min(available, target), reserve auto-grows, withdrawals pull FROM the reserve; engine at the safe-reserve calc, UI = Reserve Mode dropdown 3rd option, D11 full; **superseded same day by the AUTO SCHEDULE â€” operator: "all automatic, not me putting 40000 manually"**: `reserve_mode="schedule"` + `reserve_schedule="10000:8000, 25000:17500, 50000:27500, 100000:40000, 150000:50000, 250000:70000, 500000:100000"` â€” âœ… SHIPPED **ON** (engine walks the v3 table itself via the same tier-lookup as the lev schedule; below $10k â†’ no reserve = full balance, so inert today; between milestones the reserve absorbs ALL growth; withdrawals pull from the reserve and it self-rebuilds automatically â€” no config action ever needed). At each milestone: flip `working_capital_target` to the table value (mode working_capital) â€” one manual action, keeps the operator in the de-risk loop.
  - **âœ… RESOLVED 2026-06-29 â€” ATR-SPECIFIC vol-scaling is REFUTED; the de-lever lever is GLOBAL only (this schedule), NOT per-pair sizing. CLOSES the "high-ATR tail" thread â€” do NOT re-litigate.** Tested constant-$-risk sizing (size âˆ‌ 1/effective-SL, so the ATR-widened âˆ’1.20 pairs shrink to 0.58أ— to match a âˆ’0.70 trade's $ risk) on the screened pool: **total $ +$3001 â†’ +$2240 = âˆ’$761 (âˆ’25%)** for only âˆ’21% per-trade دƒ â€” and the rough geometric check shows the âˆ’25% mean hit DWARFS the دƒآ²/2 benefit, so it lowers compound growth too. Why: high-ATR is **net-POSITIVE** ($ by band: 0.47-0.80 = +$1628, â‰¥0.80 = +$1249; â‰¥0.80 wins +$1960 vs loses âˆ’$711) â†’ vol-scaling de-sizes the WINNERS more than the losers (PUMP/SUI +1.0-1.9% runners > the âˆ’1.20 losers). **The âˆ’1.20 high-ATR losses (SKYAI/MANTA/AGLD) are NOT a gap-through â€” they hit the engine's ATR-WIDENED âˆ’1.20 stop by design (`sl_atr_multiplier=1.5` capped at `sl_atr_widen_floor_pct=âˆ’1.20`), the RIGHT exit for the net-positive high-ATR runners.** They are the irreducible left-tail cost of a +EV cohort (same wall as flip-shorts / unmatched-long cell â€” winners & losers feature-inseparable). At a healthy balance the âˆ’1.20 losses are variance to tolerate.
  - **PREREQ (data, do FIRST): tail-stressed blended-pool Kelly.** Build a BLENDED long+short pool (full trade set across the curated batches, NOT flip-shorts only) and run `maximize g(e)=E[ln(1+eآ·m_i)]` with losers' fills stressed to their in-trade/post-exit troughs (paper truncates the tail at the clean SL â†’ biases Kelly HIGH). Output = growth-optimal exposure â†’ de-lever tiers. **Note 2026-06-26:** ran it on the FLIP-SHORT-ONLY 5-batch pool (N=104) â†’ e*=**0أ—** in all 3 tail scenarios because that sleeve's mean is NEGATIVE (âˆ’0.014%/trade realized, âˆ’0.636% gap-stressed, worst âˆ’10.17%) â†’ Kelly won't lever a zero-edge coin flip AT ALL. That's a verdict on the SLEEVE (de-lever the flip-short sleeve toward observation), not the account.   - **ًں“گ CAPITAL-SCALING STRATEGY (operator-chosen 2026-06-30 â€” DESIGN registered, BUILD DEFERRED until forward-validated & balance approaches the first tier; no-op at $3k).** Goal = **$1M *banked* (withdrawn), NOT $1M in-account** â†’ less ruin exposure. Three composed knobs, with the primary being the RESERVE (not the leverage curve):
>     1. **Reserve as the PRIMARY de-risk knob, reframed as "fixed working capital".** Today `reserve` is static (`reserve_percentage=20`; engine line ~2124 `tradeable = balance âˆ’ reserve`). Build a `reserve_mode="working_capital"` + `working_capital_target` ($, 0=off): `tradeable = min(available âˆ’ floor, target)`, so the reserve % **auto-grows** with balance to keep deployed capital â‰ˆ constant. WHY this over the leverage curve: our real tail is **5 CORRELATED positions stopping together** â€” reserve caps *total deployed* regardless of correlation (the leverage curve only shrinks each of the 5, still deploys all). Property: **max correlated-cluster loss stays clamped at a fixed $** (â‰ˆ working_capital أ— SL% أ— lev) no matter how big the account gets â†’ true ruin bound. e.g. $50k working cap â†’ ~$7-10k max cluster loss whether the account is $60k or $500k.
>     2. **â‡’ The balanceâ†’leverage schedule (â‘  above) then goes FLAT, not descending.** `exposure â‰ˆ (1âˆ’reserve%)أ—lev` â€” with reserve fixing working capital, a *descending* lev curve would DOUBLE de-risk (kills compounding). So with working-capital mode ON: leverage stays **constant** on the working capital (and the â‘  schedule must be re-keyed to working-capital or disabled, else it reads TOTAL balance and de-levers twice). Pick ONE primary: **reserve-primary + flat lev** (recommended, better for the correlated tail) OR the â‘  descending-lev curve with reserve 0 â€” not both aggressive.
>     3. **Periodic REAL withdrawals still required.** Reserve protects vs *trading* losses but stays ON the exchange (platform/hack risk) and doesn't *realize* the $1M. Operator's skim plan (withdraw $100k per +$150k gained) is the realize step â€” but **calibrate the early phase**: a FIXED $150k threshold makes cycle-1 from a small base require a huge % run (+1500% from $10k) with nothing banked = max ruin exposure exactly when most fragile. FIX: **(a) return the initial stake ASAP** (once ~2-3أ—, pull the original capital â†’ zero personal-ruin risk from day 1); **(b) skim proportionally early** (% of each gain), switching to the fixed $100k/$150k cadence only once the account is ~$100k+ where $150k is a sane %.
>     - **CALIBRATION (do FIRST, with data): the working_capital size is set from the forward MAX-DRAWDOWN + the correlation of the 5 concurrent positions (Nâ‰¥30 forward), NOT guessed.** Ties to the tail-stressed Kelly prereq (line ~77). Build only when balance nears the first tier.
>     4. **ًں“ڈ CAPACITY CEILING is the second calibration input (operator-ratified 2026-07-01 â€” "de-lever vs fixed $50k volume" resolved: SEQUENCED, fixed cap is the ENDGAME).** The strategy has a market-dictated max size: the edge (+0.2-0.4%/trade net) scalps thin alts and is fragile to slippage, which grows with order size â€” somewhere ~$10-30k/position marginal slippage eats the marginal edge, and no capital fixes that. So: de-lever/ramp = the transition; **fixed working capital (â‰ˆ fixed max tradable volume) = the destination** â€” it aligns with the real constraint, makes drawdown-% shrink automatically as balance grows (ruinâ†’0), and is one revisable number vs a schedule to mis-tune. **Do NOT pick the cap a priori ($50k is a placeholder): measure it from `exit_slippage_pct` telemetry as size scales (slippage-vs-notional curve; cap where marginal slippage eats â‰¥~30% of the per-trade edge).** The binding calibration wins: min(risk-based cap from DD+correlation [pt 3], capacity cap from slippage). Linear in-account growth at the ceiling is FINE â€” wealth realizes via the withdrawal plan (pt 3), not in-account compounding. Want more than the ceiling? â†’ a SECOND strategy (the parked BTC 4h Donchian module), never more size on this one.
- **â‘، Server-side reduce-only stop-market backstop (closes the bot-outage gap-tail hole) â€” 2026-06-26.** Live SL is currently a SOFTWARE/monitored stop (bot watches WS price â†’ fires market order w/ 3أ— bounded retry); NO resting exchange-side stop â†’ a bot/WS outage or violent gap has no server-side safety net (the `protective_sl_order_id` column is vestigial/unwired). FIX: place a reduce-only STOP_MARKET on Binance at open so the exchange closes near the level even if the bot dies. **âڑ  HISTORY: attempted before and REMOVED â€” it generated Binance errors on close trades** (likely reduce-only/qty/precision conflict with the bot's own market close racing the resting stop). So a re-attempt MUST solve the dual-close race (e.g. cancel the resting stop in the close path before the bot's own market close, or make the resting stop the SOLE close mechanism for SL exits). Not a paper concern (paper fills the SL clean at trigger, ~0 slippage); strictly a live-hardening item. The everyday live fill is ~SL+slippage (â‰ˆâˆ’1 to âˆ’1.5%), NOT the âˆ’4.77% worst-case trough; the resting stop closes the rare violent-gap/outage tail.

- **ًں”­ WATCHLIST (2026-06-17) â€” generalize the BE-ratchet to the NORMAL realtime trailing (active, decoupled breakeven floor).** Root cause of VELVET-type round-trips (armed peak +0.76 â†’ âˆ’1.20 SL): the realtime trailing pullback trigger is ATR-FLOORED (`_effective_pullback = max(base, entry_atr أ— trailing_atr_multiplier=0.5)`), so on a high-ATR pair (VELVET ATR 1.59%) the give-back needed to ARM the trail is huge â†’ it never crosses while in profit (`trailing_first_pullback_pnl_pct = âˆ’1.094` = first crossing was already at âˆ’1.09%) â†’ the ATR-widened hard SL is the only exit. **`trailing_min_profit_to_fire`=0.1 does NOT cover this** â€” verified at [trading_engine.py:9127](services/trading_engine.py:9127) it's a SUPPRESSOR (cancels an already-triggered trailing close below 0.1, flips-only), the OPPOSITE of a floor â€” it removes exits below 0.1, never creates one, and it's COUPLED to the ATR-pullback trigger that didn't fire in time (on VELVET it even suppressed the âˆ’1.09 close â†’ SL took it to âˆ’1.20). **PROPOSAL: an active, DECOUPLED BE-ratchet on the realtime path** â€” once `running_peak â‰¥ be_arm (0.45)`, force a close at `pnl â‰¤ be_lock (0.10)` regardless of the ATR-pullback (`reason TRAILING_BE_RATCHET`). Fixed P&L level â†’ immune to the high-ATR scaling problem; direction-agnostic (covers flip-longs AND the short side as a backstop). VELVET: would exit ~+0.10 vs âˆ’1.20 (saves ~+1.30); shadow_tight (0.25 P&L give-back) +0.51 confirms a fixed floor works. Config: `trailing_be_ratchet_enabled` + `trailing_be_arm_pct=0.45` + `trailing_be_lock_pct=0.10`. **SCOPE decision pending: flips-only (lower blast radius, where the gap is seen) vs all trailing trades.** Caveat: caps a dip-then-rerun at the lock (bounded â€” banks a small win; lower the lock for more room). Note: this is the GENERAL version of the SHORT runner BE-ratchet already shipped (which is ATR-floor-specific + short-only).

- **ًں”€âڑ ï¸ڈ FLIP CHAIN-POSITION BUG â€” WATCHLIST (identified 2026-06-15, NOT fixed; decision deferred to data).**
  **CORRECT DESIGN (the intent):** the flip should fade ONLY entries that *passed every filter and would have actually traded* but for the fan dead-zone â€” i.e. genuine "would-have-opened" longs (fan 0.85-3.00 / 5.0-99) and shorts (fan 1.00-1.90). For that, `FAN_RATIO_GATE` must be the **LAST** gate in the chain, so a fan-blocked entry is guaranteed to have cleared all other filters.
  **ACTUAL DESIGN (what's coded):** `FAN_RATIO_GATE` fires at **gate #8 of ~27** in `scan_and_trade` (line ~6771), and the flip opens *right there* â€” BEFORE ~19 downstream gates (`BTC_TREND_FILTER`, `BTC_SLOPE_*`, `BTC_1H_*`, `BTC_ACCEL_CHASE_LONG`, `PAIR_TREND_FILTER`, `VOL_GATE`, `BREADTH_GATE`, PAIR_ATRâ€¦). So flips fade a **contaminated SUPERSET**: entries that passed only the first 8 filters, NOT all of them. A fan-blocked long that would have failed a downstream gate (e.g. NEAR â€” a counter-trend bullish stack in a HEALTHY_BEAR that `BTC_TREND_FILTER`/`PAIR_TREND_FILTER` would likely have killed) still triggers a flip today. (Does NOT change which entries *trade* â€” fan-band entries are always blocked either way â€” only which ones *flip*; the phantom seeds at the same wrong point, so its +0.13% edge is on the superset too.)
  **COUNTERINTUITIVE TWIST (why not fixed blindly):** the downstream gates block *counter-trend* entries, so the "junk" longs they'd block are exactly the ones whose fade (SHORT) is **macro-aligned** (short with a bear) â€” and those won this batch (NEAR +0.40% pk, FARTCOIN +0.63% pk, N=2 = noise). The passed-all-filters longs are in *supportive* regimes â†’ their fades are counter-trend-into-the-trend (the cohort steamrolled in STRONG_BULL). So fixing blindly might drop the WINNERS and keep the losers.
  **DECISION GATE (resolve with data, target Nâ‰¥30 clean flips): deeply evaluate flip WINNERS vs LOSERS â€” primarily by REGIME ALIGNMENT (macro-aligned fade vs counter-trend fade, using captured `entry_macro_trend`/`entry_btc_regime`) and the Entry-Conditions-by-Outcome separators.** â‘  If a CLEAR loser-filter emerges (e.g. counter-trend fades lose, aligned win) â†’ **KEEP the current mid-chain design and ADD that filter** to remove the losers (a regime-gate, NOT a chain move). â‘، If NO clean separator emerges â†’ **revert to the CORRECT design: move `FAN_RATIO_GATE` + the flip trigger + the phantom seed to the END of the filter chain** (after `BREADTH_GATE`, before `open_position`), so flips only fire on genuine passed-all-filters entries â€” and re-validate the edge on the clean cohort. Until resolved: keep mid-chain (more volume = faster N for the split); cost is low (flip on 1أ— probation, net-negative regardless).
- **ًں”€ًں§ھ REGIME-ALIGNMENT FINDING + FAN_CONTROL / FAN-RATIO-CURVE EXPERIMENT â€” shipped 2026-06-15 (phantom/observation-only, forward-only).** **THE FINDING (mechanism-backed, from the 2-batch flip split):** flip winners vs losers separate cleanly on **macro regime alignment, NOT the FAN signal.** A fade that aligns with the BTC EMA20 slope wins (aligned: ~88% WR / +$126 in-sample); a counter-trend fade loses (short into a RISING BTC: ~50% WR / âˆ’$120). Smoking gun = FARTCOIN: same pair, won its fade in a bear window, lost the SAME fade twice in a bull window. **Open question this experiment answers:** is the fan dead-zone (0.85-3.00/5.0-99 long, 1.00-1.90 short) actually *doing* anything, or is it incidental to regime alignment? **Two probes added:** â‘  **FAN_CONTROL phantom** â€” a virtual fade seeded when an entry's fan ratio is OUTSIDE the dead-zone (i.e. the entry PASSES the fan filter); it's the A/B control for FAN_RATIO_GATE â€” if FAN_CONTROL fades pay the SAME as FAN_RATIO_GATE fades (once regime-matched), the fan band earns nothing and the real signal is pure regime. Seeded in the fan gate's `for-else` branch (loop completes with no band match â†’ fan outside dead-zone), fail-silent, never affects live. â‘، **FAN-RATIO CURVE** â€” a new `ًں”€ Phantom Flip` sub-table (`#phantom-fan-curve-body`, both text exports) that pools FAN_RATIO_GATE + FAN_CONTROL phantoms and buckets by fan ratio (0-0.85 / 0.85-1.0 / 1.0-1.35 / 1.35-1.65 / 1.65-2.0 / 2.0-3.0 / 3.0-5.0 / 5.0-99) أ— regime alignment (all / aligned / counter), flagging which buckets are in the dead-zone (DZ). Goal: find WHERE the aligned edge peaks across fan ratio â†’ **define the best fan range for fades** (refines or replaces the dead-zone for the flip sleeve). **READ at Nâ‰¥30 pooled fades/bucket: if the aligned edge is flat across ALL fan buckets (DZ and non-DZ alike) â†’ the fan band is incidental; design the live flip sleeve as a pure REGIME-ALIGNMENT gate (fade only when macro-aligned, any fan). If the aligned edge concentrates in specific fan buckets â†’ tighten the flip's fan range to those. Either way the live regime-alignment gate (deferred above) gets its fan window from this curve.** Friction wall still applies: phantom is frictionless, live pays ~0.27%/trade â†’ +0.30% promotion bar on any bucket before it ships live.

## Known risks
- **Gross 30أ— tail**: a âˆ’3.3% correlated gap â‰ˆ âˆ’100% equity (per-position SLs are primary protection; gross cap is flash-crash insurance).
- **Multiplier amplification on fat-tail losers**: C6/C1/W2 cohorts are 62-74% WR *winners* net-dragged by a few 3أ—-amplified losers â†’ fix is surgical sizing on the specific losers, NOT blocking the cohort ("high-WR-but-net-losing" trap).
- **LONG book structurally weak** (negative in most cross-batch dimensions); LONG vol floor occasionally clips high-ATR runners.

- **SHORT volume rescue stays $0** (mirroring LONG $50M would un-block dead-tape SHORTs like SEI).
- **Don't add more entry filters reflexively** â€” 15+ already, diminishing returns. Exit-side + sizing is the active lever.
